Parsing & Compilation Phase\\n**Key File**: `sc/source/core/tool/compiler.cxx` and `sc/inc/compiler.hxx`\\n**Key Class**: `ScCompiler` (extends `formula::FormulaCompiler`)\\n\\nThe compiler takes a formula string like `=SUM(A1:A10)` and tokenizes it into a bytecode representation (token array). The `ScCompiler` class:\\n- Parses the formula using formula::FormulaCompiler's tokenization engine\\n- Handles various address conventions (A1, R1C1, etc.)\\n- Resolves named ranges and external references\\n- Produces a `ScTokenArray` (bytecode) that the interpreter can execute\\n\\n### 2. Formula Cell Storage Phase\\n**Key File**: `sc/inc/formulacell.hxx` and `sc/source/core/data/formulacell.cxx`\\n**Key Class**: `ScFormulaCell`\\n\\nThe `ScFormulaCell` class represents a single cell containing a formula. It:\\n- Stores the token array (formula bytecode) in member variable `pCode`\\n- Maintains dirty/recalc state via flags like `bDirty`, `bCompile`, `bTableOpDirty`\\n- Caches the last computed result in `ScFormulaResult aResult`\\n- Tracks formula dependencies for listening/broadcasting\\n- Supports formula groups for vectorized calculation of multiple cells with the same formula\\n- Implements the `Interpret()` method that triggers evaluation\\n\\n### 3. Recalculation Scheduling Phase\\n**Key Files**: `sc/inc/document.hxx`, `sc/source/core/data/documen7.cxx`\\n**Key Class**: `ScDocument` (which manages recalculation state and scheduling)\\n**Key Enum**: `ScRecalcMode` (defined in `include/formula/tokenarray.hxx`)\\n\\nThe recalculation system:\\n- Uses `ScRecalcMode` flags to determine when cells need recalculation:\\n  - `ALWAYS`: Always recalculate\\n  - `WHEN_STORED`: Recalculate when stored (default)\\n  - `MUST_AFTER_IMPORT`: Must recalculate after import\\n  - Others: Control volatile functions, conditional recalc\\n- Maintains a formula tree (doubly-linked list) of all formula cells via `pFormulaTree` and `pEOFormulaTree` pointers in `ScDocument`\\n- `ScDocument::PutInFormulaTree()` adds cells to the recalc queue\\n- `ScDocument::CalcFormulaTree()` iterates through the formula tree and recalculates dirty cells\\n- Tracks dependencies through listeners/broadcasters for automatic recalculation\\n\\n### 4. Interpretation/Evaluation Phase\\n**Key File**: `sc/source/core/inc/interpre.hxx` and `sc/source/core/tool/interpr*.cxx` (8 files)\\n**Key Class**: `ScInterpreter`\\n\\nThe interpreter evaluates the compiled token array:\\n- Spans 8 implementation files (interpr1.cxx through interpr8.cxx) due to size\\n- `ScInterpreter::Interpret()` is the main entry point that walks the token array\\n- Implements all built-in functions (SUM, AVERAGE, IF, etc.) as individual methods\\n- Maintains an operand stack for intermediate values during evaluation\\n- Handles type conversions between numeric, string, and array values\\n- Returns results that are cached in the `ScFormulaCell`\\n\\n### Execution Flow Example: `=SUM(A1:A10)`\\n\\n1. **Compilation** (compiler.cxx):\\n   - Formula string `\\\"=SUM(A1:A10)\\\"` is parsed\\n   - Tokenized as: [OP_SUM] [OP_RANGE A1:A10]\\n   - Stored as token array in ScTokenArray\\n\\n2. **Storage** (formulacell.cxx):\\n   - ScFormulaCell created with the token array\\n   - Cell marked as `bDirty = true`\\n   - References to A1:A10 registered as listeners\\n\\n3. **Scheduling** (documen7.cxx):\\n   - Cell added to formula tree via `PutInFormulaTree()`\\n   - When A1 or any cell in A1:A10 changes:\\n     - Dependent cell is marked dirty\\n     - Added to formula tree for recalculation\\n   - `CalcFormulaTree()` is called to recalculate all dirty cells\\n\\n4. **Evaluation** (interpr1-8.cxx):\\n   - `ScInterpreter::Interpret()` executes token array\\n   - SUM function handler collects values from A1:A10\\n   - Computes sum and returns numeric result\\n   - Result cached in `ScFormulaCell::aResult`\\n   - Cell marked as clean (`bDirty = false`)\\n\\n### Key Design Patterns\\n\\n- **Lazy Evaluation**: Formulas are only recalculated when marked dirty\\n- **Dependency Tracking**: Formula cells listen to their referenced cells\\n- **Token Array Caching**: Compilation is cached in ScFormulaCell to avoid recompilation\\n- **Formula Grouping**: Multiple cells with the same formula can share the token array\\n- **Incremental Recalc**: Only dirty cells are recalculated via the formula tree\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":532,"cache_read_input_tokens":48136,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":532},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"4dd395f2-b395-405a-a8ba-fdec57cab89b","uuid":"04846dca-4bb0-484a-bb8d-c95e507852c7"}
